<div id="review_1396336083" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1396336083" />
    <a title="Cameron Wiggins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6102286-cameron-wiggins"><img alt="Cameron Wiggins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471842064p2/6102286.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1396336083?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cameron Wiggins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cameron Wiggins" href="/user/show/6102286-cameron-wiggins">Cameron Wiggins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6102286-cameron-wiggins?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396336083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3599683780548201357">Robert Dugongi has written a very good police procedural/legal thriller. It took me awhile to realize this about My Sister’s Grave. It didn’t come to me right away that I was reading a very good novel. Dugongi’s writing style is a bit loose and somewhat quirky. It is definitely a book that you have to give yourself to. I am a fan of police procedurals and legal thrillers so I would be more apt to like My Sister’s Grave. <br/>Tracey Crosswhite grew up in the Cascade Mountain area of Washington State i</span>
  <span id="freeText3599683780548201357" style="display:none">Robert Dugongi has written a very good police procedural/legal thriller. It took me awhile to realize this about My Sister’s Grave. It didn’t come to me right away that I was reading a very good novel. Dugongi’s writing style is a bit loose and somewhat quirky. It is definitely a book that you have to give yourself to. I am a fan of police procedurals and legal thrillers so I would be more apt to like My Sister’s Grave. <br />Tracey Crosswhite grew up in the Cascade Mountain area of Washington State in the small town of Cedar Grove. Her sister went missing 20 years earlier and was eventually killed. The whole town seemed to change. Cedar Grove lost its innocence. A previously convicted rapist, Edmond Parker was found to be the perp and incarcerated for the crime. Tracey went to college, came back to Cedar Grove and became a chemistry teacher. She teaches for one year and realizes that she is still too close to her sister’s death. She moves to Seattle and joins the police force and eventually becomes promoted to homicide/violent crimes.<br />Tracey’s character is extensively developed, in fact, considerably more than any other character. The only character developed even close to as much as Tracey is the defense attorney. The perp is portrayed almost as a clown. Perhaps, this is all on purpose. I am very much into character development, plot, and storyline. These elements are not that critical to Dugoni, which doesn’t make for a bad book, necessarily. Dugoni employs personal flashback chapters in italics quite a bit to tie his story together, and it works. One thing that I can say about this book, is that to me, the pace of the book remains fairly constant and then starts amping up towards the end. This cannot be said of a lot of legal thrillers or police procedurals as so many details need to be included to piece the story together later. But, this is just my opinion about the pace of the book.<br />Anyway, 20 years have passed and Tracey’s sister’s body is discovered. New evidence is now present. Does the state have the right man locked up? Tracey has her doubts, but what she really wants to know is how did her sister die? A conspiracy appears to be amidst.<br />Although this book may be quite different to a lot of people, it is still a very good book. Dugoni has done a fine job with this book. I think that My Sister’s Grave will appeal to a vast audience of readers that read legal thrillers or police procedurals. 4 stars.<br /><br />I would like to thank Amazon and NetGalley for a copy of this book for my honest review.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3599683780548201357" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094027819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2188805021705634436">Absolutely excellent! This is a thriller at its best for me. I kept flicking the pages and ended up staying up very late [early hours of the morning and tired out the next day] to finish reading it. It so captured every single tingle in me. <br/><br/>For 20 years she has been wondering what has happened to her sister. For 20 years she believes the wrong person was blamed. No body to proof anything. I can't tell you too much about this story as it needs to be read by you the reader to get all the pieces of</span>
  <span id="freeText2188805021705634436" style="display:none">Absolutely excellent! This is a thriller at its best for me. I kept flicking the pages and ended up staying up very late [early hours of the morning and tired out the next day] to finish reading it. It so captured every single tingle in me. <br /><br />For 20 years she has been wondering what has happened to her sister. For 20 years she believes the wrong person was blamed. No body to proof anything. I can't tell you too much about this story as it needs to be read by you the reader to get all the pieces of the jigsaw puzzle, but I tell you this in all honesty, the last piece of the jigsaw puzzle was a right shocker for me. Had me fooled.<br /><br />There is a nice love interest in among this which was nice to see among all the drama. I tell you, many times I was biting my nails and sitting on the edge of my seat. This author can sure tell a story well that kept the graphic and pictures running in my minds eye, I went every step of the way with this one.<br /><br />I will be seeking out more of Robert Dugoni's books if they are good as this one.<br /><br /><i> I really want to thank Amazon Publishing via Net Galley for my copy of this great fantastic thriller, without access to it I may have missed a truly amazing read <i></i></i></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4jdRD5OqIO22CiC83kZG6gOCakCRpALDbms0tnNm6MjYETjdKPTphREhlN0ps0w11d2NiF8pjKQ1FXIHviUaUg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+DAO84OZQfpHn+h9zjxiKQ57ZxPt/7x33dA95DkHMevCFmchOMeIkuC0XBw5yWj22CSA2yNyMhCGrntV9ETDcQ==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4236988298113499508">Robert Dugoni is the New York Times, #1 Amazon, and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling Author of the Tracy Crosswhite series: My Sister's Grave, Her Last Breath, In the Clearing, The Trapped Girl and Close to Home, A Steep Price and A Cold Trail as well as the short prequels The Academy and Third Watch. The police procedural featuring Seattle Homicide Detective Tracy Crosswhite has kept Dugoni in </span>
  <span id="freeText4236988298113499508" style="display:none">Robert Dugoni is the New York Times, #1 Amazon, and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling Author of the Tracy Crosswhite series: My Sister's Grave, Her Last Breath, In the Clearing, The Trapped Girl and Close to Home, A Steep Price and A Cold Trail as well as the short prequels The Academy and Third Watch. The police procedural featuring Seattle Homicide Detective Tracy Crosswhite has kept Dugoni in the Amazon top 10 for more than three years and sold more than 5 million copies. He is also the author of the critically acclaimed The Extraordinary Life of Sam Hell, released April 2018 and soon to be a major motion picture. He is also the author of the Charles Jenkin's International spy series, The Eighth Sister and The Last Agent, soon to be a television series. Dugoni's first series featured attorney David Sloane and CIA agent Charles Jenkins. <br />He is the winner of the Nancy Pearl Award for fiction, a two-time nominee for the Harper Lee Award for Legal Fiction, A two-time nominee for the Mystery Writer's of America Edgar Award and a two-time nominee for the International Thriller of the year. His non-fiction expose, The Cyanide Canary, was a 2004 Best Book of the Year. He is published in more than 30 countries and two dozen languages.<br />You can sign up for his newsletter at:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.robertdugoni.com">http://www.robertdugoni.com</a> and message him on facebook, twitter and instagram </span>
  <a data-text-id="4236988298113499508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
